  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_b08f8b9e-7c81-47b2-a654-78311e2085d1'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer532711958380481025">On May 15, 1975, fifteen-year-old Ginny Lemon is abducted from a convenience store in Fort Lauderdale by a member of one of the most notorious and brutal motorcycle gangs in South Florida. <br/> <br/>From that moment on, her life is forever changed. She gets a new name, a new identity and a new life in the midst of the gang’s base on the edge of the Florida Everglades—a frightening,</span>
  <span id="freeText532711958380481025" style="display:none">On May 15, 1975, fifteen-year-old Ginny Lemon is abducted from a convenience store in Fort Lauderdale by a member of one of the most notorious and brutal motorcycle gangs in South Florida. <br /> <br />From that moment on, her life is forever changed. She gets a new name, a new identity and a new life in the midst of the gang’s base on the edge of the Florida Everglades—a frightening, rough and violent world much like the swamps themselves, where everyone has an alias and loyalty is tantamount to survival. <br /> <br />And at the center of it all is the gang’s leader, Grizz: massive, ruggedly handsome, terrifying and somehow, when it comes to Ginny, tender. She becomes his obsession and the one true love of his life. <br /> <br />So begins a tale of emotional obsession and manipulation, of a young woman ripped from everything she knows and forced to lean on the one person who provides attention, affection and care: her captor. Precocious and intelligent, but still very much a teenager, Ginny struggles to adapt to her existence, initially fighting and then coming to terms with her captivity. <br /> <br />Will she be rescued? Will she escape? Will she get out alive—or get out at all? Part psychological thriller, part coming-of-age novel, filled with mystery, romance and unexpected turns, Nine Minutes takes readers into the world of one motorcycle gang and inside the heart of a young girl, whose abduction brought about its fall.</span>
  <a data-text-id="532711958380481025" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

Nothing else was changed.)</i><br/><br/>I am having a hard time qualifying my thoughts on this book. That being the case, I also went back and forth all night about what I wanted to rate it. You'll notice I said <i>all night</i> </span>
  <span id="freeText11559477277586430022" style="display:none"><b>12/4/16: Holy crap, This is <u>FREE</u><br>Just wanted to let people know so they don't miss the deal...this was my favorite read of 2014, I can't recommend it enough. <br><br>It fucked me up for days...<br><br>--5 Gripping Grizz Stars--</b><br><br><br><i>***Spoiler Free***<br><br>(Updated 1/10/15 to include disclaimer at the end of my review. Nothing else was changed.)</i><br><br>I am having a hard time qualifying my thoughts on this book. That being the case, I also went back and forth all night about what I wanted to rate it. You'll notice I said <i>all night</i> as this was me...all last night:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415721231ra/11834799.gif" width="384" height="288" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Which never happens. <br><br>Because I'm typically verra unfeeling and cold-hearted, quite honestly.<br><br>It takes a <i>lot</i> for a book to hit me in the feels. <br><br>And even more to make me cry. In fact, only this book and <i>Transcendence</i> by Shay Savage have ever made me done so. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415721231ra/11834800.gif" width="500" height="231" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>But seriously.</b> <br><br>This book legit kept me up because I couldn't stop thinking about it. And when you have to get up at 4am every day, that's really saying something. In fact, I can't remember the last time a book affected me so much. <br><br>Now I'm not saying that I loved everything that happened in this story, because I sure as hell didn't. Indeed, there were some parts I fucking <b>hated</b>, especially toward the end. <br><br>But this book was compelling as fuck people. <br><br>Therefore, 5 thousand huge stars. <br><br>I'm going to keep this review somewhat short and vague, because there was a lot going on in this story and I don't want to inadvertently include any spoilers.<br><br>Let's begin... <br><br>This was me 2% in:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415721231ra/11834801.gif" width="250" height="179" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And the remaining 98%...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415721231ra/11834802.gif" width="250" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415721231ra/11834803.gif" width="500" height="376" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415721231ra/11834804.gif" width="540" height="375" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415721451ra/11834844.gif" width="635" height="464" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415721231ra/11834806.gif" width="250" height="185" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415721231ra/11834807.gif" width="250" height="132" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415721570ra/11834872.gif" width="500" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415721231i/11834809.jpg" width="300" height="222" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415721231ra/11834810.gif" width="250" height="141" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415721231ra/11834811.gif" width="250" height="107" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415721231ra/11834812.gif" width="400" height="198" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And that was this book for me in a nutshell. <br><br><u>Some Reading Advice:</u><br><br>-<b>DO</b> limit the amount of reviews you read on this book - unless they specify spoiler free. <br><br>Before reading this, I quickly skimmed maybe 2-3 reviews, one of which included a spoiler that wasn't tagged as such, which I noticed...but didn't really <i>notice</i> until it came up in the book. Go in as blind as possible. The blurb is enough. <br><br>-<b>DON'T</b> expect a classic romance and a classic HEA.<br><br>I wouldn't really call this book a romance. Yes, there is definitely a love story element here, but if you are reading this with the expectation of a traditional romance book with steamy sex scenes, you will be sorely disappointed. <br><br>-<b>DO</b> expect to completely hate OR completely love - or perhaps both - one of the main characters. <br><br><b>DON'T</b> read this book at all if you have issues with underage characters being involved in possible sexual situations with adult characters.<br><br>This is obviously alluded to in the blurb, but I stress this because I know this is a sticking point for some people. <br><br><b>
  <u>Final Thoughts:</u>
</b><br><br>I thought this book was amazing, although I can see some people outright hating it due to some of the subject matter and/or the path the story takes as well as its conclusion. <br><br>I went into this book not knowing that it was a part of a series. As such, while there <i>is</i> a sense of closure at the conclusion of this story, it is definitely not all inclusive. You are left with <i>a lot</i> of unanswered questions. So much so, in fact, that some people might view this as a bit of a cliffhanger. <br><br>The writing was superb. I loved how the author laid this thing out. It is told via first person narrative, from the past and about the past, with a hefty dose of foreshadowing. <br><br>Think <i>Forrest Gump</i> / <i>Shawshank Redemption</i> style narration. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415723866i/11835231._SX540_.jpg" width="540" height="288" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In short, this is perhaps the most powerful thing I've read in years. <br><br>And so in the spirit of that I say, rid yourself of any reservations and "Run Forrest, Run" to get this book.<br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415723824ra/11835221.gif" width="500" height="211" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Random Disclaimer: In recently re-reading this review, I saw that I have a Bill Cosby Jello gif in here and I just wanted to let everyone know that I wrote this review WAY before the whole possible Cosby/rape scandal came to light...I just wanted to throw that out there in case anyone was thinking I purposefully included that, what with any possible relation to the story's subject matter.</i> </span>
  <a data-text-id="11559477277586430022" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1103064829" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1103064829" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1103064829?book_show_action=true">Nov 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=book-1-of-my-fav-series">book-1-of-my-fav-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1103064829" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7634638615126721052"><b>::: FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ::: 5 STARS!!! :::</b><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415748292i/11839963.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411226198ra/11208601.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>WOW!! I was completely blown away by this book!! </b> It was a dark, gritty, dangerous, intense, shocking, addictive, raw, and captivating page-turner. A complex, multi-layered story with <i>outstanding</i> writing and unexpected twists and turns!!  I could <u>not</u> put it down for even a minute!! If you're looking for a well-written, intense, and utterly <em>unputdownable</em> book with a completely unique and original plot, and a surprising love story that'll captivate you </span>
  <span id="freeText7634638615126721052" style="display:none"><b>::: FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ::: 5 STARS!!! :::</b><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415748292i/11839963.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411226198ra/11208601.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>WOW!! I was completely blown away by this book!! </b> It was a dark, gritty, dangerous, intense, shocking, addictive, raw, and captivating page-turner. A complex, multi-layered story with <i>outstanding</i> writing and unexpected twists and turns!!  I could <u>not</u> put it down for even a minute!! If you're looking for a well-written, intense, and utterly <em>unputdownable</em> book with a completely unique and original plot, and a surprising love story that'll captivate you from the very first page, <b>READ THIS!!!</b><br><br>I officially have an EPIC book hangover!! 5 STARS!!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>On May 15, 1975, fifteen-year-old Ginny Lemon is abducted from a convenience store in Fort Lauderdale by a member of one of the most notorious and brutal motorcycle gangs in South Florida.<br><br>From that moment on, her life is forever changed. She gets a new name, a new identity and a new life in the midst of the gang’s base... And at the center of it all is the gang’s leader, Grizz: massive, ruggedly handsome, terrifying and somehow, when it comes to Ginny, tender. She becomes his obsession and the one true love of his life.</b>
</blockquote><br>Wow, right?<br><br>At this point, I was pretty sure I had a idea what direction the story was heading. Then I opened the book and read the prologue. <em>Wait... what??!</em> Did that really just happen?? O.O -- At that point, there was no turning back for me. I just <em>had</em> to know this story and see what could possibly have led them to that place. The interesting thing was that I ended up surprised by what I felt -- and I loved that! This book made me think I was going to feel one thing, then showed me how I actually felt something <em>entirely different.</em><br><br>I don't want to say anything about the plot other than what the blurb tells you, because honestly, that's all you should know. It's quite a complex storyline with a lot of layers and it's best to just let them unfold as you read. From beginning to end though, I could not look away even for a minute. It was one jaw-dropping scene after another and I couldn't flip the pages fast enough.<br><br>This is just one of those books that you can't stop reading.<br><br>The writing was absolutely phenomenal. Vivid, evocative, and utterly captivating. This was a full length book (326 pages) but I  just <em>flew</em> through it in an afternoon. There was an ease and fluidity to the language that gave the story no stopping points. It was fast-paced but focused on all the right details. I can't say enough good about this author's writing style. Honestly, it's some of the best I've read.<br><br>Is there a cliffhanger? Will there be a sequel? -- First of all, I was completely happy with this ending. <u>It was the ending I wanted</u>. I do not consider this a cliffhanger. This chapter of the story is over. However, there is more to the story to tell... so there will be a sequel coming in Spring 2015. My strong advice though is to read this now and don't wait. I honestly was left in a good place.<br><br>It's actually very rare for me to read biker books and the simple reason is that there's a lot about their lifestyle that is just a little too "much" for me to handle reading about. But I <em>loved</em> this book. It was not graphic. Yes, there was all sorts of sex, violence, cold-blooded brutality, but it was not graphic, nor was it over-dramatized. It was not erotic, in fact the sex was all fade-to-black, it was there as a fundamental part of the story but it wasn't the driving force. The writing just let you know what was happening, and often that would be chilling enough to build a vivid picture in your mind without needing further details.<br><br>Addressing the issue of age... Yes, she is underage. She's about 15-16 at the start. There is no violent rape. Grizz genuinely cares for her. That being said, what happens is still wrong. My guess is that Grizz is about 30(ish) so yep, that's uncomfortable. But you've read the blurb... this isn't meant to be a fluffy book.<br><br>Another thing is don't go looking for spoilers. I've been asked so many questions by readers that start with "<em>Omg, I heard that....*spoiler*.... happens. Does it</em> <em>really??</em>"<em> </em>and honestly my answer is that you have to just see how it unfolds because what you think its going to be, isn't what it is. But if I tell you what it is, then that'll ruin everything. And you guys know that I'll often do spoiler pages whenever I think it's best to know stuff in advance but this is a case where I really feel it's best to just let the story happen.<br><br>Lastly, based on what I've seen of reader reactions to the prologue, it seems there are two types of reactions. The first kind are the ones who <em>LOVE</em> it and dive right in. To you guys, I say: <em>YAY!! Go for it!!! Enjoy the crazy ride and come tell me what you thought when you're done!!</em> .... But there's another group of readers who read the prologue and kinda go WTF and nope right out of the book. To you guys, I'll say this: <em>Yes, it's exactly what it looks like... <u>but it's not at all what you think</u>. There are so many twists and the  book reveals the true complexity of the situation. My advice is <u>don't assume anything</u><em> before you know the full story because, as you read, your feelings might change... I know mine sure did!</em></em><br><br><strong>Guys, this is an absolutely fantastic book. One of the best I've read. I highly recommend it!!</strong><br><br><strong>Rating: 5 STARS!!</strong><br><br>_______________________________________<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="7634638615126721052" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1103121155?book_show_action=true">Nov 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Christy by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1103121155" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17318395296274885459"><b>5 stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/b483819d-689e-40c2-a8a1-fbe44809f06c_zpsf2c185c4.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420624733i/13246021.jpg' alt=' photo b483819d-689e-40c2-a8a1-fbe44809f06c_zpsf2c185c4.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>For me, a good book is a book you enjoy reading. You look back and think, I liked this book or this character. A great book is a book you remember. It’s a book that touches you, with characters you adore. A exceptional book is a book you can’t stop thinking about. A book that stays with you for days. A book that makes you think, makes you feel, and changes how you think and feel. This was an exceptional book for me. Did I love everything about it? No. But I couldn’t put it down. It’s</span>
  <span id="freeText17318395296274885459" style="display:none"><b>5 stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/b483819d-689e-40c2-a8a1-fbe44809f06c_zpsf2c185c4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420624733i/13246021.jpg" alt=" photo b483819d-689e-40c2-a8a1-fbe44809f06c_zpsf2c185c4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>For me, a good book is a book you enjoy reading. You look back and think, I liked this book or this character. A great book is a book you remember. It’s a book that touches you, with characters you adore. A exceptional book is a book you can’t stop thinking about. A book that stays with you for days. A book that makes you think, makes you feel, and changes how you think and feel. This was an exceptional book for me. Did I love everything about it? No. But I couldn’t put it down. It’s been days and I’m still reeling over what I’ve read. I have all these feelings and I just don’t think I’ll ever forget this book. I’ll never forget the characters, the story, and how it made me feel when I was finished reading.<br><br>Meet Ginny Lemon, also know as Kit. A fifteen year old girl who was abducted by a biker. A girl who’s life was forever changed in one moment. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/e668d7bf-27d7-426a-a1c1-8b679d1ffa91_zps42c099ae.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420624698i/13246016.jpg" alt=" photo e668d7bf-27d7-426a-a1c1-8b679d1ffa91_zps42c099ae.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>I was a loner but never lonely.</blockquote>
</b><br>This girl was my favorite character of the book. I can’t imagine being that age, being taken from everything I’ve known and placed into somewhere like this biker compound. But she takes it in stride. She’s strong. She’s determined to make the best of everything. <br><br>When she first meets Grizz, she doesn’t know what to think of him. He’s older than her, he’s a biker, and even though she doesn’t want him to know it, she’s terrified at first. Grizz is not a perfect man. Not even close. But he does care for Kit. He loves her and he has his reasons for the things he’s done and the way he chose to do them. He’s rough, he’s tough, but with Kit, he has a sweet and gentle side. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/58d52544-6dd3-467f-8c1a-e3a2d47c4666_zps589431ac.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420624698i/13246017.jpg" alt=" photo 58d52544-6dd3-467f-8c1a-e3a2d47c4666_zps589431ac.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>With time, Kit adjusts to living in this world. Though she never is truly comfortable with all the things that goes on around her, these people become her friends and family. She makes friends with a girl named Moe and a guy named Grunt who is about her age. Their friendship makes things easier for her. She’s accepted the way her life is, and in some ways she loves it. She loves Grizz. But loving him makes her question herself. <br><i>
  <blockquote>He was my first love. He was a true love.</blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/d2fd2b71-e19c-4e35-84e0-7df3b6883f73_zps99964f86.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420624698i/13246018.jpg" alt=" photo d2fd2b71-e19c-4e35-84e0-7df3b6883f73_zps99964f86.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I don’t want to say much more about the story line. There are so many unpredictable twists and turns and by the end, my jaw was on the floor. Everyone will have their theories, their questions and their speculations. Hopefully the sequel that comes out in spring will answer all our questions. This book doesn’t have a cliffhanger, it just leaves things open. And I need this second book. I have to see what’s going on. <br><br> Nine Minutes is not a feel good book. It’s not a sweet and sexy romance. There is love, there are some elements of romance, but if you’re looking for something light and fluffy this is not the book for you. It’s raw. It’s gritty. It’s got characters that have such strength and determination. It’s not your run of the mill biker book. It’s unique. It captivated me from the start and I couldn’t put it down. Nine Minutes is an unconventional love story that I know I’ll never forget. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/efa302c7-beee-432b-a02e-3bba603262c3_zpsad561316.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420624698i/13246019.jpg" alt=" photo efa302c7-beee-432b-a02e-3bba603262c3_zpsad561316.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="17318395296274885459" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1102082796" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1102082796" />
    <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei"><img alt="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421992465p2/2551178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1102082796?book_show_action=true">Nov 09, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei">Lady Vigilante (Feifei)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=i-trust-my-friends">i-trust-my-friends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=bikers">bikers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=historical-schmorical">historical-schmorical</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=dark-taboo-forbidden-reads">dark-taboo-forbidden-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=i-love-my-friends">i-love-my-friends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=douchenugget">douchenugget</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=this-is-for-ana">this-is-for-ana</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1102082796" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9234809892628267293"><b>5 stars!!!!!</b><br/><br/>If there can only be one book you can get this month, heck, even this year, it <b>
  <u>HAS</u>
</b> to be this one. This is going to sound cheesy, but I felt so alive when I was reading this book. It’s a story that evoked visceral reactions, put me in a book frenzy, and made me feel like I was taking caffeine shots. This book was 200% unputdownable for me. I’m a very paranoid and picky reader and unless a book has positive reviews from my friends (because we know each other’s tastes well) I won’t</span>
  <span id="freeText9234809892628267293" style="display:none"><b>5 stars!!!!!</b><br /><br />If there can only be one book you can get this month, heck, even this year, it <b>
  <u>HAS</u>
</b> to be this one. This is going to sound cheesy, but I felt so alive when I was reading this book. It’s a story that evoked visceral reactions, put me in a book frenzy, and made me feel like I was taking caffeine shots. This book was 200% unputdownable for me. I’m a very paranoid and picky reader and unless a book has positive reviews from my friends (because we know each other’s tastes well) I won’t pick it up. However, this book’s synopsis had my attention and for the rest of the day I couldn’t stop thinking about it. I read a sample which was the engrossing prologue that gave me goosebumps and after that I was a goner. Putting down the book just simply wasn’t an option. Pages were flipped, tears were shed, and 2 hours later I was done.<br /><br />The rest of my review is going to be a bit unconventional. There is SO much in this book so I decided to do a Q&amp;A review. You see, every time I worked on my review, I would get a question, a message, or a comment asking me this and that and it really made me see that my normal review style is just not going to be good enough to cover everything. So the rest consists of questions others have asked me and my thoughts without spoiling anything.<br /><br /><u>
  <b>Is there romance and an HEA?</b>
</u><br /><br />That is the most asked question and my answer is yes to the romance. 100% yes. But I also have to say that if you are a romance only reader, this book may not be for you. As for the HEA part, I can’t emphasize enough that because this book crosses many other genres, we can’t subject it to the same kind of scrutiny as we do for pure romance books. So that HEA question? Hold onto it. It’s not defined and is something every reader has to decide for themselves. But for me personally? It was the best kind of happy ending that stayed true to both the characters and the story.<br /><br /><u>
  <b>What genre is this book?</b>
</u><br /><br />It’s not one specific genre. It crosses over many sub-genres as well and this is what I think the book falls under:<br /><br />-MC <br />-Dark<br />-YA<br />-Psychological thriller<br />-Romance<br />-Historical (referring to the setting)<br />-Religious (referring to the heroine’s faith)<br /><br />After mulling it over, I think it was faulty of me to project this book as mainly a biker book first. The heroine’s life does revolve around a motorcycle club but it’s not what defines her. Her age makes this book YA, her kidnapping, attitude, and psyche makes this a psychological thriller, her twisted love for a dangerous man makes this a romance, and the gritty biker life portrayed that has many triggers makes this dark. And speaking of triggers…<br /><br /><u>
  <b>Yes, there are triggers in this book!!</b>
</u><br /><br />Ginny is 15 when she’s taken. It honestly made me uncomfortable to know that our heroine is underage, probably because I have a younger sister close to her age and it makes me sick to think of an abduction like this ever happening to her. I will also be frank and say there is a questionable rape scene present and it was the first time in the book where I cried. The circumstances revolving around this scene is what made my heart break for all parties involved. And violence…yes, there is a good amount of violence, and a few scenes where it’s in explicit detail. But never did I feel like anything was gratuitous. Everything said and done had a purpose.<br /><br /><u>
  <b>How historical is this book besides the setting?</b>
</u><br /><br />Well the story spans from the time Ginny was kidnapped in 1975 to the year 2000 where a monumental trial takes place. 25 years of history packed in this story. I also want to point out that just because this book has a MC background, don’t expect it to be like other ‘modern’ biker books. You really can’t compare a present day MC to one 20-30 years ago. Times are different and people change. <br /><br /><u>
  <b>Cheating, love triangle, and sex</b>
</u><br /><br />With all honesty, I can’t say there was or wasn’t cheating or a love triangle because my opinion is not a fact. My opinion is no, there was no cheating and no love triangle (those needing details will have to message me), but for others even a tiny detail will make the difference in deciding if lines have been crossed. The sex is fade to black. This is not your typical MC where all guys act like manwhores and all girls are skanks. Sex in here is not meant to get you hot and flustered; it’s meant to drive an emotional impact home. <br /><br /><u>
  <b>Is this a mindfuck?</b>
</u><br /><br />200% yes. From the beginning to the very end, I felt like I was smacked upside down with plot twists. This story was so unpredictable, the characters unstable (some even volatile), and the psychological aspect added an extra layer of complexity to it all. Even now, I am still questioning whether the romance in here was more obsession or love. I think it’s both. An obsession turned into love and on the flip side where love for another turns into an obsession. If anything, the latter is confirmed with the revelation near the end of the book.<br /><br />For me, this aspect was the most compelling. I think there are just some events, some things words are not enough to explain or account for, and the love/obsession is a prime example. You really have to experience it, feel it, to have a point of reference.<br /><br /><u>
  <b>Cliffhanger, standalone, and series info</b>
</u><br /><br />Once again, these topics are all subjective and opinion vs. fact. It is a fact that this is a series and book 2 will focus on these same characters. It is my opinion that this book doesn’t have a cliffhanger but of course I know some will say otherwise. The book has a full beginning, middle, and end and is very much a complete story, but the ending doesn’t resolve all the loose ends. That closure will be seen in the next book. But at the same time, even if there wasn’t a second book I would be completely satisfied with the way this one ended.<br /><br />So yeah…this book is quite complex and difficult to explain in just a few words. I am still finding it hard to believe this is a debut novel. I can’t remember the last time a debut book has completely blown me away like this one did. I can undoubtedly say that this is a book that has it all. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>Pre-review</i>
</b><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[This is one of the BEST books I've ever read, and probably my favorite biker book. Ever. I'm in such a book frenzy I can't calm down soon enough to gather my thoughts and write a review just yet, but anyone with eyeballs should pick this book up NOW. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>
  <a data-text-id="9234809892628267293" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText2460901921573461760" style="display:none"><b>Full review now posted </b><br><br><b>5–Unsettling–Stars <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416203511i/11911658._SX540_.jpg" width="375" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>First Impressions – 11/16</u></b><br><br>Wow!   <u>Update – 11/25</u>
</b><br><br>Well, it's been over a week since I've read this book and I've spent the whole time trying, but failing, to finish this review. I just wasn't having any luck expanding on what I already posted. FINALLY, IT DAWNED ON ME THAT MY REVIEW WAS ALREADY DONE. There was nothing left for me to say. I had already expressed my feelings and the affect this book had on me. <br><br><i>Nine Minutes</i> is one of the best book I've read this year. Why? Because even a week later, I'm still thinking about it. I'm still affected by it. I'm still obsessing over it. This story made a huge impression on me like few books have. If that isn't good writing, I don't know what is. <br></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1103140454" class="readable"
              >

  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418815761i/12909722.png' alt=' photo nineminutescollage.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>

I basically had to throw almost every single one of my morals out the window for this book. <b> And I can't stop thinking about it. </b><br/>I'm not an avid reader of all of the mindfuck books, but I know this isn't the usual mindfuck that readers of that genre expect. (Btw sorry for the excessive use of </span>
  <span id="freeText4275555003568898252" style="display:none">12/2/16 Kindle freebie!!! <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/2gwyyd6">http://amzn.to/2gwyyd6</a><br>---------------------------------------<br><br><b> 5 stars! </b><br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/nineminutescollage.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418815761i/12909722.png" alt=" photo nineminutescollage.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b> Fuck it. I'm giving this 5 stars. </b> This was the most morally conflicting book I've read in a long time. I basically had to throw almost every single one of my morals out the window for this book. <b> And I can't stop thinking about it. </b><br>I'm not an avid reader of all of the mindfuck books, but I know this isn't the usual mindfuck that readers of that genre expect. (Btw sorry for the excessive use of the word "fuck" but it's helping me process this book).<br><br>Ginny is 15 years old when a biker offers her a ride home. Instead of bringing her to her house, he drives her to the Satan's Army compound, where she discovers that she's being offered as a gift to the head honcho Griff. Ginny is given a new name, Kit and told to basically forget about her life before the MC. <br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/Untitled.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418857558i/12924017._SX540_.png" alt=" photo Untitled.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>For my own poor brain, I'm going to have to break this review down by character.<br><br><b> Ginny/Kit: </b> One thing I keep reading in other reviews is how surprised people are that she didn't try to escape despite a few opportunities to do so. When you look at where she came from, with a mother and a stepfather who weren't cruel, but didn't really seem to care about her I can kind of understand how she decided to stay. At the club, she had people who cared about her (albeit in their own sick and twisted way) but she really wasn't ignored or neglected like she had been at home. <br><br>Ginny without a doubt had Stockholm syndrome. There's really no denying it, but what I thought was interesting was how she ignored all of the bad things in order to remain somewhat sane. Every time she saw something horrible or heard about it after the fact it was a huge emotional trauma. So I sort of don't blame her for choosing to remain oblivious when it was a survival skill kicking in.<br><br><b> Grizz: </b> This is the man who brought out all of my morally conflicted thoughts when reading this book. Was Grizz a bad guy, the villain? Yes. Did he treat Ginny horribly? <b> NO. </b> In fact, Grizz never really hurt Ginny directly. She ended up being hurt because of him, but he always treated her well and with respect (except for one instance but it was explained later). Grizz may not have been the hero of the story, but he could have been much much worse of a man to Ginny considering all of his other crimes.<br><br>I couldn't help but compare him to other MC leaders in popular books. I don't usually compare books to each other, but comparing these characters with Grizz really helped me make up my mind about whether or not I liked him.<br> Now don't go and stab me with your pitchforks ladies, but I HATED Tack from Motorcycle Man. He was technically a "good" guy but he treated his woman like shit and ordered her around and she just took it. Did Griff do this to Ginny? No. The only orders he gave her were for her safety. And for almost all of their relationship, he put Ginny's wellbeing ahead of his.<br><br>The other character I wanted to compare Grizz to was Deuce from Undeniable. Another MC guy that I fucking HATED because guess what? he treated his woman like shit and cheated on her all the time. In Undeniable the age difference is very much present, like 20 years or something and it was gross. I liked that in this book, we know the age difference is great, but it's never explicitly stated. So for me, it wasn't that gross because I could picture a guy 10 years older than Ginny instead of 20 or 30 years older (vomits).<br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/Untitled.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418857558i/12924017._SX540_.png" alt=" photo Untitled.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>One of my favorite realizations when reading this book was the absolute devotion Grizz had for Ginny. He knew that he took her, and that legally he could be punished for it. Grizz lived every day knowing that he could lose Ginny. The police could come and take her, she could try to run away, someone would eventually recognize her. The worst being his actions could scare her away from him. But he loved her, so he did his best to treat her well and to show her how he felt. He knew he had to appreciate her while he had her.<br><br>I will warn that there are many triggers in this book. There is rape, murder, torture, and other difficult content. But I feel like if I could stomach it, you could because normally these issues are hard limits for me. Just know that this is a story like no other, so give it a chance.<br><br><i> Thanks Feifei for recommending this one to me! </i><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="4275555003568898252" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1109245683" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1109245683" />
    <a title="Cristina Monica" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14596170-cristina-monica"><img alt="Cristina Monica" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1589617514p2/14596170.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1109245683?book_show_action=true">Nov 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cristina Monica" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cristina Monica" href="/user/show/14596170-cristina-monica">Cristina Monica</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=abuse">abuse</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=love-triangle">love-triangle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=dark">dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=bikers">bikers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1109245683" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17029406197481806617"><b>*3.5 stars*</b><br/><br/>Not bad. Not bad at all. There may have been some elements in the story that I couldn’t help but frown at but, overall, I was absorbed.<br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416294160i/11932070.png' width='500' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The beginning of the story is somewhat frustrating. A fifteen-year-old girl being abducted and living among dangerous men and women? And she doesn’t try her best to escape? What kind of person would give up so fast? Well, let me tell you that it took me quite some time to come to understand the main character. I did comprehend her motives but, at the </span>
  <span id="freeText17029406197481806617" style="display:none"><b>*3.5 stars*</b><br><br>Not bad. Not bad at all. There may have been some elements in the story that I couldn’t help but frown at but, overall, I was absorbed.<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416294160i/11932070.png" width="500" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The beginning of the story is somewhat frustrating. A fifteen-year-old girl being abducted and living among dangerous men and women? And she doesn’t try her best to escape? What kind of person would give up so fast? Well, let me tell you that it took me quite some time to come to understand the main character. I did comprehend her motives but, at the same time, I couldn’t stop thinking about her parents that, yes may be alcoholics, but seemed to love her very much nonetheless. Also, I know that her parents could probably have been killed if she escaped and my mind tells me that she did do, in a way, the right thing by staying there, except I cannot believe that she became friendly to others so fast. And it’s like she wasn’t conscious of where she was all the time. That is mainly what bothered me the most about this story. It’s not an easy subject, I understand, and it’s personal to everyone, indeed, but I think the author could have tried to make the main character look more vehement to find a way of getting her life back. And don’t trust Grizz that easily.<br><br>Wow, I really didn’t expect there to be a love triangle. But, to be honest, it didn’t bother me at all. While I may not have always believed into Grizz and Ginny’s love for each other, it was obvious to me that Grunt and her had a remarkable connection. He was the sweetest and acting like a gentleman with her. Grizz, on the other hand, was taking good care of her and gave her whatever she needed – except for her freedom – and that made him a little hard to not like him. He can be very very awful with people, especially those who have betrayed him or did him wrong. Ginny wasn’t okay with everything Grunt did, so that made it some better. Overall, the romance had its qualities and was intriguing, but it did lack a bit of realism.<br><br>The secondary characters were great! I truly found them unique and excellent in their role. It does happen often that I encounter characters that feel like a thousand others I have met before, but, with this, it was not the case. There was also this atmosphere that made me think of a ship with pirates, except, less loud. The secondary character I loved most was Moe. She was so fantastic. You know when you read a certain book, there is always this not-so-important character that stands out to you and you can’t help but notice and want her/him to be more present in the plot? That’s how I felt with Moe. She’s there when it makes sense to the plot, I agree, but I still couldn’t help but want more of her.<br><br>The writing wasn’t astonishing or the equivalent, but it was good. Pleasant enough, even though I did feel like there was no special style. It was standard, I shall say.<br><br>I guess the reason I read this book so quickly and was hooked by it was because of the plot, which was very addictive. There was always something happening that you couldn’t help but react at and say ‘‘OMG.’’ Although, the ending did not please me. There was this revelation I was not ready for and it completely took me by surprise. But not in the positive sense of things.<br><br>If you’re fervently into dark contemporary romance stories containing notorious bikers, I would recommend this with all my heart! But if this is not something you think might please you, then I cannot say it is worth your time. It was good and I mean it, but I am not tremendously excited to read the sequel.<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="17029406197481806617" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1102390327" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13914948224940594047">This book was amazing! I could not put it down. This story gripped me on page one and didn't let go till the very end. Prepare to have your mind blown!<br/><br/>Kidnapped at 15 by outlaw bikers, Ginny (aka Kit), soon finds herself falling hard for Grizz, the leader of the biker gang who has been obsessed with Ginny for years. The deeper she falls and the longer she lives in the midst of this outlaw world, the more conflicted she feels about Grizz. Her love for him is strong, but she cannot reconcile the c</span>
  <span id="freeText13914948224940594047" style="display:none">This book was amazing! I could not put it down. This story gripped me on page one and didn't let go till the very end. Prepare to have your mind blown!<br /><br />Kidnapped at 15 by outlaw bikers, Ginny (aka Kit), soon finds herself falling hard for Grizz, the leader of the biker gang who has been obsessed with Ginny for years. The deeper she falls and the longer she lives in the midst of this outlaw world, the more conflicted she feels about Grizz. Her love for him is strong, but she cannot reconcile the cold-blooded killer with the gentle man that loves her so fiercely. Nor can she ignore her attraction to Grunt, the young man that becomes her friend and her sanctuary over the years.<br /><br />Despite the reality of how Kit came into her relationship with Grizz, she grows to genuinely love him and their life together. If you're expecting a tale of abuse and Stockholm Syndrome with a "victimy" feel, you won't get it here. Brace yourself for a love story of epic proportions. <br /><br />This book went far beyond my expectations. Just when I thought I had it all figured out, Ms. Flynn turned my world upside down! There is so much of this story left to be told that I can hardly contain myself. Please let the second book in this series be available as a pre-order. I need it STAT! <br /><br />This book is definitely a new favorite of mine! Click it. Buy it. Read it. You won't regret it!</span>
  <a data-text-id="13914948224940594047" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1104335539" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1104335539" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1104335539?book_show_action=true">Nov 12, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/22839067-nine-minutes">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1104335539" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4828994274822814041"><br/><b>4.5 Stars</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>”Missing Girl Found Married to Leader of Notorious Motorcycle Gang.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span> <br/><br/>This is one well done page turning debut novel. This story starts with a heart pounding prologue that takes place at an execution. The author then takes a reader on a kidnapping tale of fifteen year old Guinevere Love Lemon by the Satan’s Army motorcycle gang from the years 1975 to 2000. The story was fast paced and the twists and turns that are gifted at the end will leave a reader going over events i</span>
  <span id="freeText4828994274822814041" style="display:none"><br><b>4.5 Stars</b><br><br><b>
  <i>”Missing Girl Found Married to Leader of Notorious Motorcycle Gang.”</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span> <br><br>This is one well done page turning debut novel. This story starts with a heart pounding prologue that takes place at an execution. The author then takes a reader on a kidnapping tale of fifteen year old Guinevere Love Lemon by the Satan’s Army motorcycle gang from the years 1975 to 2000. The story was fast paced and the twists and turns that are gifted at the end will leave a reader going over events in their minds on a continuous loop. <br><br>Since this book is told from a young girl’s pov of her kidnappers we don’t get any information on what these bikers are into and it seems that there are only six members, half of which have full time jobs (phone company, professor, college student, etc.??) outside of the club. Kit is never around the pit or any meetings of the clubs dealings and so I’m interested to see just what Grizz and gang were really up too.<br><br>Kit accepts and settles in (too quickly for my tastes) with her new family. The warmth of Grizz the head of this dangerous mc gang has her feeling wanted and loved for the first time in her life. <br><br><b>
  <i>”Time to meet your new family.” Maybe he was right. Maybe I was meant to be with Grizz. The realization stunned me.”</i>
</b><br><br>Kit slowly falls in love and accepts her life as Grizz's girl. She also has a strong attraction/bond with Grunt and together they keep a secret from Grizz. <br><br><b>
  <i>”If it could be, would you want it? Would you want me?”</i>
</b><br><br>Kit has many opportunities to flee her new life. Blame it on Stockholm syndrome or just acceptance but she is happy with the love and protection of Grizz. <br><br><b>
  <i>”Actually, he spoiled me rotten. Grizz was quiet. He didn’t’ talk a lot, but he was affectionate.”</i>
</b><br><br>As the years pass Kit even attends college, makes friends and lives a happy life with Grizz until the story comes full circle and we reach the prologue scene and beyond. Leslie Cowan a reporter is writing an article and before the story comes to a close many twists are revealed. <br><br>Overall, this story was an entertaining and thought provoking tale with some twists you’ll never see coming.<br><br><b>
  <i>”Can’t you give me something else here? Something to shock my readers?”</i>
</b><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="4828994274822814041" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer11371516661446224028"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br/><br/>So I've been very busy lately mainly with work but yesterday morning I said good morning to Feifei like I always do and one of the first things she said to me was, "I think you'll like this other book I just finished." <br/><br/>So immediately I was all ears because believe it or not, Feifei rarely says this to me! So I was all over it!<br/><br/>And this is my face when I finished the prologue:<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1402610180ra/9960207.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>And this is my face when I finished reading the book.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405478878ra/10403625.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Nine Minutes, is written like an autobiography and for the mo</span>
  <span id="freeText11371516661446224028" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br><br>So I've been very busy lately mainly with work but yesterday morning I said good morning to Feifei like I always do and one of the first things she said to me was, "I think you'll like this other book I just finished." <br><br>So immediately I was all ears because believe it or not, Feifei rarely says this to me! So I was all over it!<br><br>And this is my face when I finished the prologue:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1402610180ra/9960207.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And this is my face when I finished reading the book.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405478878ra/10403625.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Nine Minutes, is written like an autobiography and for the most of the book I actually thought it was because it honestly felt like the author was telling me about her life and experiences. The heroine is 15 years old when she's taken and this isn't one of those glamourised kidnapped books where the villain waits until the girl is legal before he has his way with her. Grizz was a hard man, brutal and cruel but when it came to Ginny he became a different man. But only for her. <br><br>What happened in this book was messed up, the characters were even more messed up but I ate that shit up! I think part of the allure was the writing, from the first page you kind of know how it's all going to end but not quite.<br><br>Okay I'm gonna stop babbling. FULL REVIEW TO COME.<br><br>So if you're looking for something different then you should definitely try this book! Now about that happy ending, in my opinion this book has a happy ending. But for a more thorough review, you should check Feife's review out though :D<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1102082796?book_show_action=false&amp;page=1">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420086ra/833320.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_1103033404" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1103033404" />
    <a title="Pam" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13865261-pam"><img alt="Pam" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1374039144p2/13865261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1103033404?book_show_action=true">Nov 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pam" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pam" href="/user/show/13865261-pam">Pam</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/22839067-nine-minutes">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=5">5</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=darkerside-mindfuckery">darkerside-mindfuckery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=suspense-chills-n-thrills">suspense-chills-n-thrills</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=steamy-hawt">steamy-hawt</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=fucked-up-n-broken">fucked-up-n-broken</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=biker-mc">biker-mc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=not-a-typical-kinda-love">not-a-typical-kinda-love</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1103033404" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8334812406176079564"><i>5 angsty-tangled-in-knots stars</i><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>He was my first love, He was a true love.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416980490i/12143763.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/> <br/><b>DAMN it all to hell!</b> I can't even go into detail with this book or else I'll give it all away. But I can share how this book made me feel, because this book drew out so much feelings in me that by the end I was glad it was over because I was all tied up in knots. <br/><br/>This book isn't erotic, not much sex actually, which is okay, because this book had everything else; power, greed, obsession, pain, torture and a reall</span>
  <span id="freeText8334812406176079564" style="display:none"><i>5 angsty-tangled-in-knots stars</i><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>He was my first love, He was a true love.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416980490i/12143763.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><b>DAMN it all to hell!</b> I can't even go into detail with this book or else I'll give it all away. But I can share how this book made me feel, because this book drew out so much feelings in me that by the end I was glad it was over because I was all tied up in knots. <br><br>This book isn't erotic, not much sex actually, which is okay, because this book had everything else; power, greed, obsession, pain, torture and a really really good mind fuck!<br><br>From the prologue on, I knew I was gonna hate how this book was going to make me <i>feel</i>, because I would be the first to admit that I would be the one to romanticize the situation and root for a happily ever after. <br><br>Like our brave little heroine, I survived this book only by pretending it all didn't happen, I had my blinders on only to have it ripped away in the end. I'd like to think that it helped me though, the blinders, because I was able to (stupid or not) find <i>beauty</i> in their little fucked up world and wish for them a better tomorrow. <br><br>As much as it killed me in the end, I'm glad the author went with the direction she did, because it gave an overall realness to the entire story. She didn't introduce us to hell and put a pretty red bow on it and pass it on as a happy story. It needed it <i>all</i>.<br><br>I'm really fighting with myself if I will read the next book or not. I don't think I can handle more, but at the same time that damn curiosity of where can it go from here is leading me towards, "yes". There is an ending and I am okay with the ending, because in a way in nine minutes it did end, but there is so much more to come.<br><br>Awesome read, highly recommended if you want some crazy-ass-butterflies banging away in your stomach. It felt like I was reading with one hand over my eyes and peaking through my fingers. If you know me I love a good mind fuck, hate angst but in some cases such as this I do put my big girl panties on and dive right in. If you do read this, I do recommend you have a light, funny book to follow it up wit, it will help with the post read hangover. <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="8334812406176079564" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1103345028" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1103345028" />
    <a title="~ Becs ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2626261-becs"><img alt="~ Becs ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388693144p2/2626261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1103345028?book_show_action=true">Nov 11, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/22839067-nine-minutes">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=biker-hero">biker-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=gamma-hero">gamma-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=dark-angsty">dark-angsty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=tattooed-hero">tattooed-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=abused-heroine">abused-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=kidnapped">kidnapped</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1103345028" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12322982631643163068"><b>4.5 shocking stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416155218i/11903677._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo nineminutesquotey_zpsffde1eef.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I’m really not one for MC books these days. After a fantastic beginning the genre is, at least for me, awash with mediocrity and I never normally choose to read one of these books but this one has been gathering five star ratings from reviewers I really respect so I thought it was definitely time to break the habit and go with the flow just to see what all the fuss was about.<br/><br/>I will agree that this is a highly accomplished debut from Beth Flynn and bears no resemblance to the ge</span>
  <span id="freeText12322982631643163068" style="display:none"><b>4.5 shocking stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416155218i/11903677._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo nineminutesquotey_zpsffde1eef.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I’m really not one for MC books these days. After a fantastic beginning the genre is, at least for me, awash with mediocrity and I never normally choose to read one of these books but this one has been gathering five star ratings from reviewers I really respect so I thought it was definitely time to break the habit and go with the flow just to see what all the fuss was about.<br><br>I will agree that this is a highly accomplished debut from Beth Flynn and bears no resemblance to the generic MC romance that floods my newsfeed at Goodreads daily. Yes, there is love to be found in this novel but no, it is most definitely not a romance. It’s just not told that way – it reads far more like an autobiography, a recount of information rather than a novel. The style is actually pretty spartan – there’s no flowery prose or superfluous adjectives to romanticise the story. It’s told in an incredibly matter of fact way – this is what happened, this is what I did, this is what I knew and what I didn’t. This of course helps it to stand out from the crowd and gives it a very different feeling from pretty much anything else that I’ve read this year to date.<br><br>I’m not going to give away any plot details in this review – the blurb states pretty much all you need to know. It serves you better not to know anything more as you can allow the surprises and shocks to have the full impact the author intended. And so we begin with a heart-thumping, highly evocative prologue which foretells the end of the book and will pretty much leave you agog and then we immediately go back in time to 1975, when it all began.<br><br>The story is then told by Ginny as she slowly recounts the events that lead towards the inevitable conclusion. Everything is slowly revealed and I think it serves well to pay close attention to the details here – it’s all very significant as everything begins to line up and we draw closer to the impending tragic ending as foreshown by the prologue.<br><br>I absolutely devoured this book – two train journeys disappeared in the blink of an eye as I lost myself in this story. It’s completely engrossing and captivating and refreshingly different and highly original. It’s definitely not your typical MC – the deadly biker gang is more background rather than the device that drives the story. This is Ginny’s story and she keeps herself pretty aloof from the gang most of the time. There are several ‘triggers’ in this story that may bother some readers such as underage sex, rape and strong violence but it’s not at all gratuitous and it’s respectfully done and very much adds to the whole ‘retelling of information’ style of the story.<br><br>If I have any criticisms at all it’s that much of the story focuses on the early years and as we span decades, I felt not enough time was given to the later years although this is possibly intended by the author as the epilogue gives away a few little gems of information that beg for expansion and will no doubt make up the sequel. Also, Ginny refers to her ‘husband’ multiple times during the story as a kind of mystery but I worked out who he was right from the early chapters.<br><br>Other than that, this was a truly excellent offering from Beth Flynn – hard to believe that it’s a debut. It’s compelling, tragic and spellbinding and, if books are judged by how hard they are to put down, then this is most definitely a winner. I can’t wait for the sequel to see where the author will take us next.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416160111i/11904576._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo nineminutesrating_zps0182ef78.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="12322982631643163068" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/22839067-nine-minutes">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1100994649" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9785902286678600605"><b>*****FIVE TEAM GRIZZ STARS*****</b><br/>{BR with Mel, Dee, Sharon, JR, and Tiff}<br/><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/4016616ba5016ebc5e5f07b64d74d967_zps4e803101.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/><br/><br/>This is definitely one <b>AMAZING</b> story!!<br/>I'm still reeling from the ending and teaser into the next book!<br/>I've got so many questions and all I can say is...<b>I NEED BOOK TWO NOW!!!</b><br/><br/><br/><br/>The story of Kit and Grizz is far from conventional and yes, maybe how it all started might have seemed inappropriate if you take into consideration their age difference, but I don't know, I just didn't have an issue with it.<br/><br/><br/><br/>Guinevere Love Lemon aka "</span>
  <span id="freeText9785902286678600605" style="display:none"><b>*****FIVE TEAM GRIZZ STARS*****</b><br>{BR with Mel, Dee, Sharon, JR, and Tiff}<br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/4016616ba5016ebc5e5f07b64d74d967_zps4e803101.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416888924i/12100274._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 4016616ba5016ebc5e5f07b64d74d967_zps4e803101.jpg" width="365" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>This is definitely one <b>AMAZING</b> story!!<br>I'm still reeling from the ending and teaser into the next book!<br>I've got so many questions and all I can say is...<b>I NEED BOOK TWO NOW!!!</b><br><br><br><br>The story of Kit and Grizz is far from conventional and yes, maybe how it all started might have seemed inappropriate if you take into consideration their age difference, but I don't know, I just didn't have an issue with it.<br><br><br><br>Guinevere Love Lemon aka "Kit", is kidnapped at the age of 15 and given to the President of the Satan's Army MC as a present. This is what we are led to believe but nothing is as it seems in this story!! Nothing happens by chance and my mind is literally blown away!<br><br><br><br>I loved Kit and her spunky attitude. She grew up with two negligent parents. They never abused her but they also failed to provide her a loving family environment. <br><br><br>Grizz comes off as the scary and sometimes "psychotic" Prez of the outlaw "Satan's Army" MC, but when it comes to Kit, he is the sweetest, most loving man I've ever come across in a book. I found it easy to fall <b>HARD</b> for him.<br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/ed0a1ff50ed1ff4d95b972d91a2775e6_zps516946ee.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416888924i/12100275._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo ed0a1ff50ed1ff4d95b972d91a2775e6_zps516946ee.jpg" width="365" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><br>I don't want to go into detail about this one because I think it is best to go in blind. All I can say is after getting deep into the story, I kept thinking back to the Prologue, and my heart was breaking over and over again. <b>BUT</b> the last chapter, plus sneak peek into the next book, have completely left me feeling <b>MIND FUCKED</b>!! Nothing is as it seems!!! Trust no one, people!!!!!<br><br><br><br>I am hopeful that things will turn around in book two!! Otherwise I am going to be a complete wreck!!</span>
